Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: nail polish\\ \tt RIGHT: lip gloss\\ \tt TOP: screwdriver\\ \tt BOTTOM: spoons\\ \tt CENTER: harps\\ \tt NORTHWEST: saucepan\\ \tt NORTHEAST: highlighter\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: scissors\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: bikini\\ \tt HERE: watermelon\\ \tt THERE: spider\\ \tt NOWHERE: buttercup\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: bluebell\\ \tt INSIDE: trivet\\ \tt OUTSIDE: lizard\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start.
